# Demand Concession
demand_concession_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    construction_speed = 1.2
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                OR = {
                    THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                    THIS = { ai = no }
                }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        THIS = {
            civilized = yes
            NOT = { nationalism_n_imperialism = 1 }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = berlin_conference }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { civilized = yes ai = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                civilization_progress = 0.6
                has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
            }
            AND = {
                tag = KOR
                THIS = { primary_culture = japanese }
            }
        }
        civilized = no
        number_of_states = 2
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism NOT = { government = democracy } }
            NOT = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }

        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }

			#Player can take any state neighboring their substate
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							substate_of = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}

			#Player can take any state neighboring their satellite
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							vassal_of = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}

            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                owner = { war_with = THIS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        alliance_with = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
            continent = africa
            continent = central_africa
            continent = west_africa
            continent = east_africa
            continent = south_africa

            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        raider_group_doctrine = 1
                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }
                }
            }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
                THIS = { machine_guns = 1 }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 3000000 }
                THIS = {
                    bolt_action_rifles = 1
                    army_risk_management = 1
                }
                OR = {
                    any_owned_province = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                total_pops = 3000000
                THIS = {
                    modern_divisional_structure = 1
                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }
        } ###End of Non-African Restrictions

    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONCESSION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }

demand_concession_NI_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 1.2

    badboy_factor = 1
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 0.5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                OR = {
                    THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                    THIS = { ai = no }
                }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        THIS = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					civilized = yes
					nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = berlin_conference
						has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					civilized = yes
					has_global_flag = berlin_conference
					NOT = {
						nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
						has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
					}
				}
			}
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { civilized = yes ai = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                civilization_progress = 0.6
                has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
            }
            AND = {
                tag = KOR
                THIS = { primary_culture = japanese }
            }
        }
        civilized = no
        number_of_states = 2
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism NOT = { government = democracy } }
            NOT = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }

        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }

			#Player can take any state neighboring their substate
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							substate_of = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}

			#Player can take any state neighboring their satellite
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							vassal_of = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}

            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                owner = { war_with = THIS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        alliance_with = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
            continent = africa
            continent = central_africa
            continent = west_africa
            continent = east_africa
            continent = south_africa

            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }

# Bad Boy
rude_boy = {
    sprite_index = 28
    is_triggered_only = no
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 2
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 1.5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = yes

    can_use = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				government = proletarian_dictatorship
				THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
				relation = { who = THIS value = 1 }
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
			AND = {
				government = fascist_dictatorship
				THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
				relation = { who = THIS value = 1 }
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
			AND = {
				government = radical_republic
				THIS = { government = radical_republic }
				relation = { who = THIS value = 1 }
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
		}
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        badboy = 1
        is_disarmed = no
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }

        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes
    po_disarmament = yes
    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = WAR_RUDEBOI_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Conquest
conquest = {
    sprite_index = 2
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    can_use = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				THIS = { ai = no }
				NOT = { total_pops = 400000 }
				NOT = { number_of_states = 3 }
			}
		}
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            civilized = yes
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = {
                any_state = {
                    is_colonial = no
                    NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        government = proletarian_dictatorship
                        government = fascist_dictatorship
                    }

                }
                NOT = { number_of_states = 4 }
            }
            AND = {
                tag = SWI
                NOT = { number_of_states = 4 }
            }
        }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
                has_country_modifier = disable_conquest_cb
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }

        #AI anti-military will not use this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { NOT = { war_policy = anti_military } }
        }

        #AI will not use this when fighting for hegemony
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                    any_greater_power = {
                        war_with = THIS
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        is_culture_group = THIS
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                    }
                    THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        is_greater_power = yes
                        is_secondary_power = yes
                    }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not grab cores of allies/spherelings
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        exists = yes
                        OR = {
                            alliance_with = THIS
                            in_sphere = THIS
                            vassal_of = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #pro-military AI will not grab cores of non-existing, non-union countries
        #unless they own some cores or it's part of their culture group
        #jingoistic will also grab existing cores that they already own some of
        #fascist & communist countries are exempt from this
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = pro_military }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        is_cultural_union = no
                        exists = no
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            is_culture_group = THIS
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { war_policy = jingoism }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_core = {
                        OR = {
                            any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
                            AND = {
                                exists = no
                                is_cultural_union = no
                                is_culture_group = THIS
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 5
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONQUEST_NAME
}

# Berlin Conference
annex_africa = {
    sprite_index = 22
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 1.5

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 2

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 0

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        NOT = { has_country_flag = congo_master }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        number_of_states = 2
        THIS = {
            nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            capital_scope = { continent = europe }
            NOT = { tag = RUS }
            NOT = { tag = TUR }
            slavery = no_slavery
            OR = {
                is_greater_power = yes
                is_secondary_power = yes
            }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality }
            civilized = yes
            has_global_flag = berlin_conference
        }
        NOT = {
            tag = MOR
            tag = ALD
            tag = TRI
            tag = LIB
            tag = ETH
            tag = MAD
            tag = EGY
            has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
        }
        civilized = no
        OR = {
            capital_scope = { continent = africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = central_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }
        }
        ai = yes
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects }
            }
        }
        #Claimed colonial regions can't be conquered with this CB
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = colonial_railroading_disabled
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					THIS = { tag = POR }
					THIS = { ai = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = colonial_railroading_disabled
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					THIS = { ai = yes }
					OR = {
						#Ghana
						AND = {
							any_owned_province = {
								OR = {
									region = ASH_1909
									region = FRA_1907
								}
							}
							any_neighbor_country = {
								NOT = { tag = THIS }
								civilized = yes
								any_owned_province = {
									OR = {
										region = ASH_1909
										region = FRA_1907
									}
								}
							}
						}
						#Ivory Coast

annex_africa_full = {
    sprite_index = 21
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    always = yes

    construction_speed = 2.5

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 2

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 0

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        NOT = { number_of_states = 2 }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        THIS = {
            nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
            capital_scope = { continent = europe }
            NOT = { tag = RUS }
            NOT = { tag = TUR }
            slavery = no_slavery
            OR = {
                is_greater_power = yes
                is_secondary_power = yes
            }
              NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = claimed_africa }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = congo_award }
            civilized = yes
            has_global_flag = berlin_conference
        }
        civilized = no
        NOT = {
            tag = MOR
            tag = ALD
            tag = TRI
            tag = LIB
            tag = CYR
            primary_culture = kefficho
            primary_culture = amhara
            primary_culture = tigray

# Establish Protectorate
establish_protectorate_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 1.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {

		OR = {
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
		civilized = no
        NOT = {
			is_our_vassal = THIS
			has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			number_of_states = 2
		}
		THIS = {
            civilized = yes
			NOT = {
				nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
				has_global_flag = berlin_conference
				has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			}
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
            }
            AND = {
                tag = KOR
                THIS = { tag = JAP }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }

        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism NOT = { government = democracy } }
            NOT = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
            capital_scope = { continent = africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = central_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }

            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        raider_group_doctrine = 1
                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }
                }
            }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
                THIS = { machine_guns = 1 }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 3000000 }
                THIS = {
                    bolt_action_rifles = 1
                    army_risk_management = 1
                }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                total_pops = 3000000
                THIS = {
                    modern_divisional_structure = 1
                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }
        } ###End of Non-African Restrictions

    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_PROTECTORATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
    on_po_accepted = { tech_school = unciv_tech_school }
}

establish_protectorate_NI_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 1
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 0.8
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        THIS = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					civilized = yes
					nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = berlin_conference
						has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					civilized = yes
					has_global_flag = berlin_conference
					NOT = {
						nationalism_n_imperialism = 1
						has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
					}
				}
			}
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = post_colonial_country
            }
            AND = {
                tag = KOR
                THIS = { tag = JAP }
            }
        }
        NOT = { number_of_states = 3 }
        civilized = no
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }

        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            THIS = { war_policy = jingoism NOT = { government = democracy } }
            NOT = {
                THIS = {
                    OR = {
                        capital_scope = { continent = south_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = north_america }
                        capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        #Restrictions to non-African State conquering
        OR = {
			owner = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
            capital_scope = { continent = africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = central_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }

            NOT = { total_pops = 500000 }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 1000000 }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_logistics = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        raider_group_doctrine = 1
                        iron_steamers = 1
                    }
                }
            }

            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 2000000 }
                THIS = { machine_guns = 1 }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_directionism = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        steam_turbine_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                NOT = { total_pops = 3000000 }
                THIS = {
                    bolt_action_rifles = 1
                    army_risk_management = 1
                }
                OR = {
                    capital_scope = { is_overseas = no }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = no
                        naval_integration = 1
                    }
                    THIS = {
                        ai = yes
                        oil_driven_ships = 1
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                total_pops = 3000000
                THIS = {
                    modern_divisional_structure = 1
                    army_nco_training = 1
                }
            }
        } ###End of Non-African Restrictions
    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_PROTECTORATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
    on_po_accepted = { tech_school = unciv_tech_school }
}

    war_name = CUT_DOWN_TO_SIZE_NO_INFAMY_WAR_NAME

    can_use = {
    }

    on_add = {
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		set_global_flag = rjw_over
		clr_global_flag = russo_japanese_war
		THIS = {
			set_country_flag = rj_war_victor
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						exists = yes
						OR = {
							tag = JAP
							tag = TKG
						}
					}
				}
				owner = {
					country_event = 784527
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						exists = yes
						tag = RUS
					}
				}
				owner = {
					country_event = 784531
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Make Puppet
make_puppet = {
    sprite_index = 18
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 2.0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
		ai = yes
		total_pops = 400000
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
            OR = {
				AND = {
					total_pops = 5000000
					NOT = { has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp }
				}
				AND = {
					total_pops = 2000000
					has_global_flag = you_are_playing_mp
				}
			}
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
            war_with = THIS
            any_neighbor_country = {
                OR = {
                    vassal_of = THIS
                    substate_of = THIS
                    in_sphere = THIS
                }
            }
        }
        is_vassal = no
        is_greater_power = no
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope

    po_make_puppet = yes

    war_name = WAR_PUPPET_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        country_event = 19370
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

# Become Independent
become_independent = {
    sprite_index = 10
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    always = yes

    badboy_factor = 1
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 108

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            THIS = { substate_of = FROM }
        }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        NOT = { AND = { tag = EGY ai = yes } }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        OR = {
            FROM = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
            war_with = THIS
        }
    }

    po_release_puppet = yes
    po_add_to_sphere = yes

    war_name = WAR_INDEPENDENCE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
        add_war_goal = {
            casus_belli = make_puppet
        }
        leave_alliance = FROM
        release_vassal = THIS
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Revert from Communist Government
uninstall_communist_gov_cb = {
    sprite_index = 13
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    # Is automatically added to countries that intervened at while install_communist_gov_cb
    # so they can revert those countries government.
    constructing_cb = no

    badboy_factor = 0.5
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } }
        government = proletarian_dictatorship
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = {
                    has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                }
            }
        }
    }

    po_uninstall_communist_gov_type = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

great_war_install_democracy = {
    sprite_index = 19
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 1.5
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 30
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1
    always = yes

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            has_country_flag = in_great_war
            is_greater_power = yes
            OR = {
                government = hms_government
                government = constitutional_empire
                government = democracy
            }
        }
        has_country_flag = in_great_war
        civilized = yes
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        war_with = THIS
        OR = {
            government = proletarian_dictatorship
            government = fascist_dictatorship
        }
    }

    po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.05
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        THIS = { set_country_flag = friendly_democracy }
        country_event = 96085
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

    sprite_index = 19
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 1.5
    crisis = no

    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 50
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

                government = hms_government

                government = democracy
            }
        }
        has_global_flag = great_wars_enabled
        civilized = yes

        OR = {
            government = proletarian_dictatorship
            government = fascist_dictatorship
        }
        OR = {

            }
        }

                    has_country_modifier = no_more_war

# Gain control of Substate region
acquire_substate_region = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        num_of_substates = 1 # if has any substate
        THIS = { ai = no }
        any_substate = {
            OR = {
                neighbour = THIS
                AND = {
                    THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            number_of_states = 1
            any_owned_province = {
                NOT = { is_core = THIS }
                is_colonial = no
            }
        }
    }

    allowed_substate_regions = {
        is_colonial = no
        #owner = { NOT = { in_sphere = THIS } }
        any_owned_province = {
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
            is_colonial = no
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_SUBSTATE_REGION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Gain control of Substate Core region
acquire_substate_core_region = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no
    always = yes

    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 2.2
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1840 }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        num_of_substates = 1 # if has any substate
        THIS = { ai = no }
        any_substate = {
            any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
            #NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
            OR = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                AND = {
                    THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
                any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            }
            NOT = { in_sphere = THIS }
            number_of_states = 1
        }
    }

    allowed_substate_regions = {
        any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS }
        #NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            AND = {
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
        }
        owner = { NOT = { in_sphere = THIS } }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Dismantle fortifications (forts + naval bases)
dismantle_forts = {
    sprite_index = 16
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    badboy_factor = 1
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1


    can_use = {
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = {
                NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
        }
        THIS = { civilized = yes }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state
    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                has_building = fort
                has_building = naval_base
            }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
            }
        }
    }

    po_destroy_forts = yes
    po_destroy_naval_bases = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }


	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

#Placeholder for acquire state-by-event
acquire_any_state = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    constructing_cb = no
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 0
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

	always = no

    can_use = {
        is_vassal = no
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        #Countries can't take capitals
        NOT = {
            any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
        }

        #AI treats colonial states with only civilized cores as regular states
        OR = {
            is_colonial = no
            AND = {
                is_colonial = yes
                THIS = { ai = yes }
                any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = yes } }
                NOT = { any_owned_province = { any_core = { civilized = no } } }
            }
        }

        ###Can only grab neighboring states, coastal if it's a coastal GP
        OR = {
            #AI and Player can take a neighboring state
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }

            #Player can take a neighboring state neighboring a neighboring state
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } } }
                    }
                }
            }

            #AI/Player can take a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = {
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                    OR = {
                        is_greater_power = yes
                        is_secondary_power = yes
                        ai = no
                    }
                }
            }

            #Player can take any state neighboring a coastal state
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    any_neighbor_province = {
                        state_scope = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    ai = no
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
        }

        #AI will not try to grab cores of their union if they're sphere to a GP of their culture group
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            NOT = {
                AND = {
                    THIS = {
                        is_greater_power = no
                        part_of_sphere = yes
                        culture_has_union_tag = yes
                        cultural_union = { exists = no }
                        sphere_owner = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        any_core = {
                            is_cultural_union = yes
                            this_culture_union = this_union
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    civilized = no
                    is_culture_group = east_asian
                    OR = {
                        owns = 1481
                        owns = 1496
                        owns = 1498
                        owns = 1538
						owns = 3364
                        owns = 1566
                        owns = 1569
                        owns = 1606
                        owns = 2632
                    }
                }
                THIS = {
                    civilized = yes
                    NOT = { is_culture_group = east_asian }
                    any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                }
            }
            owner = { country_event = 1316089 }
        }
    }
}

            from = jingoism

						tag = COS
					}
				}
			}
			THIS = { badboy = -4 }
		}
		USA = { casus_belli = { target = THIS type = humiliate months = 12 } }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_culture_group = latin_american_cultures
				exists = yes
				NOT = { primary_culture = brazilian }
			}
			casus_belli = { target = THIS type = humiliate months = 120 }
			casus_belli = { target = THIS type = liberate_country months = 120 }
			relation = { who = THIS value = -400 }
			leave_alliance = THIS
		}
    }
    on_po_accepted = {
		USA = { casus_belli = { target = THIS type = free_peoples months = 12 } }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_culture_group = latin_american_cultures

conquest_any = {
    sprite_index = 22
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    constructing_cb = no
    crisis = no

	always = no

    can_use = {
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
    }

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 0
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 0
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 0
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONQUEST_ANY_NAME

    on_add = {
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        THIS = {
            random_owned = {
                limit = { is_core = TRN TRN = { exists = no has_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest } }
                THIS = { release_vassal = TRN }
                TRN = { clr_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest civilized = no annex_to = THIS }
                TRN = { civilized = yes }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { is_core = ORA ORA = { exists = no has_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest } }
                THIS = { release_vassal = ORA }
                ORA = { clr_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest civilized = no annex_to = THIS }
                ORA = { civilized = yes }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { is_core = NAL NAL = { exists = no has_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest } }
                THIS = { release_vassal = NAL }
                NAL = { clr_country_flag = uncivilize_on_conquest civilized = no annex_to = THIS }
                NAL = { civilized = yes }
            }
        }
    }
}

treaty_port_casus_belli = {
    sprite_index = 32
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 1
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 10
    penalty_factor = 2

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 4
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 4
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        THIS = {
            civilized = yes
            is_disarmed = no
            any_owned_province = { has_building = naval_base }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
            OR = {
                AND = {
                    total_amount_of_divisions = 1
                    total_amount_of_ships = 25
                    total_pops = 250000
                    rank = 16
                }
                war_with = THIS
            }
            OR = {
                NOT = { war_policy = pacifism }
                ai = no
                war_with = THIS
            }
        }
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        civilized = no
        is_vassal = no
        num_of_cities = 2
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }

            owns = 1700 #Algiers
            owns = 1704 #Oran
            owns = 1701 #Bougie
            owns = 1709 #Bone
        }
    }

    po_reparations = yes

    tws_battle_factor = 1.5

    war_name = PUNITIVE_EXPEDITION_WAR_NAME

    on_add = {

            from = jingoism

        random_owned = {

                    civilized = no

                        owns = 1569 #Weihaiwei

                        owns = 1608 #Ningbo
                        owns = 1071 #Qeshm
                        owns = 1695 #Ifni
                        owns = 2640 #Gwadar

                        owns = 2048 #Zanzibar

                        owns = 1637 #Cheju
                        owns = 2589 #Tsushima
                        owns = 3260 #Sado

                    }
                }
                THIS = {

end_radicals = {
    sprite_index = 37
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 5
    prestige_factor = 4
    peace_cost_factor = 75
    penalty_factor = 1
	always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
		THIS = {
			NOT = {
				government = democracy
				government = radical_republic
				ruling_party_ideology = radical
			}
		}
		government = radical_republic
		is_vassal = no
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
			AND = {
				has_country_modifier = francia_utopia
				THIS = { ai = yes }
			}
        }
        civilized = yes
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
    }

	po_add_to_sphere = yes
	po_remove_prestige = yes

    war_name = WAR_END_RADICALS_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.05
        }
    }

			}

				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = liberal
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled
						}
						ruling_party_ideology = liberal
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
					}
				}
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = i_am_being_unradicaled

					}

#Colonial Conquest/Imperialism CB
colonial_conquest = {
    sprite_index = 21
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 0.25
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 1
    always = yes

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
            war_with = THIS
        }
        number_of_states = 2
        NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        NOT = { in_sphere = THIS }
        civilized = no
        exists = yes
        OR = {
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 150 } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { badboy = 0.88 } }
        }
        THIS = {
            civilized = yes
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects }
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = claimed_africa }
            is_disarmed = no
            NOT = { war_policy = pacifism }
            OR = {
                AND = {
            capital_scope = { continent = europe }
                    NOT = {
                        tag = TUR
                        tag = RUS
                    }
                }
                tech_school = naval_tech_school
                tech_school = japanese_tech_school
            }
            state_n_government = 1
        }

        OR = {
            #Mozambique
            AND = {
                THIS = {

#Colonial Conquest/Imperialism Annex
colonial_conquest_full = {
    sprite_index = 21

    construction_speed = 0.8

    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }

# War Reparations
war_reparations = {
    sprite_index = 27
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 0.8

    badboy_factor = 0.2
    prestige_factor = 0.5
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        war_with = THIS
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
            has_country_modifier = no_more_war
            has_country_flag = in_great_war
        }
        THIS = {
            civilized = yes
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier }
        }
    }

    po_reparations = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME_REPARATIONS

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    tag = HAI
                    FRA = { is_greater_power = yes }
                    NOT = { has_country_flag = agreed_to_pay_debt }
                }
            }
            owner = {
                country_event = 45108
            }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    tag = MEX
                    has_country_flag = pay_1st_pastry_war
                }
            }
            owner = {
                country_event = 45108
            }
        }
    }
}

#Steal Puppet CB
steal_puppet = {
    sprite_index = 10
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.4

    badboy_factor = 1.8
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 5
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 0

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = in_great_war
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
				has_country_modifier = neutrality
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        civilized = yes
        num_of_vassals_no_substates = 1
		NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
		THIS = { ai = no }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        is_our_vassal = FROM
        FROM = { is_substate = no }
    }

	po_release_puppet = yes
    po_add_to_sphere = yes

    war_name = WAR_NAME

    on_add = {
		THIS = { clr_country_flag = picked_steal_target }
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				vassal_of = FROM
				is_substate = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = unreleasable_country }
			}
			country_event = 6016855
		}
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        THIS = { set_country_flag = new_overlord }
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

monroe2 = {
    sprite_index = 19
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no
    constructing_cb = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 15
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    always = yes

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            tag = USA
            government = democracy
            is_greater_power = yes
            has_country_flag = shield_NW
        }

            capital_scope = { continent = europe }

USS_monroe = {
    sprite_index = 19
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    crisis = no
    constructing_cb = no

    always = yes


    badboy_factor = 0.5
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 0.5
    penalty_factor = 0.5

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        THIS = {
            has_country_flag = formed_USS
            is_greater_power = yes
            has_country_flag = USS_miranda
        }
        OR = {
            is_culture_group = american_cultures
            is_culture_group = neo_european_cultures
            capital_scope = { continent = europe }
            capital_scope = { continent = africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = west_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = asia }
            capital_scope = { continent = oceania }
            capital_scope = { continent = australia_new_zealand }
            capital_scope = { continent = polynesia }
        }
        any_owned_province = {
            OR = {
                continent = south_america
                continent = north_america
            }
            any_core = {
                OR = {
                    primary_culture = mexican
                    primary_culture = central_american
                    primary_culture = north_andean
                    primary_culture = south_andean
                    primary_culture = platinean
                    primary_culture = brazilian
                    primary_culture = caribeno
                    primary_culture = afro_latino
                    primary_culture = afro_brazilian
                }
            }
            NOT = {
                is_core = THIS
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        NOT = { tag = FROM }
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = FROM
            NOT = { has_global_flag = the_call_for_south_american_union }
        }
        FROM = {
            OR = {
                primary_culture = mexican
                primary_culture = central_american
                primary_culture = north_andean
                primary_culture = south_andean
                primary_culture = platinean
                primary_culture = brazilian
                primary_culture = caribeno
                primary_culture = afro_latino
                primary_culture = afro_brazilian
            }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state

    war_name = WAR_LIBERATE_NAME

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = FROM
            OR = {
                continent = north_america
                continent = south_america
            }
        }
    }

        country_event = 2651    # Territorial Loss event

    }

        }

#Take Capital
take_capital = {
    sprite_index = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12
    construction_speed = 0.5

    badboy_factor = 3
    prestige_factor = 10
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 36

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1

    can_use = {
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                #THIS = { ai = yes }
                has_global_flag = sw_set
                NOT = { year = 1840 }
            }
        }
        THIS = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = in_great_war
                has_country_modifier = no_more_war
                has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
            }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        number_of_states = 2 # annex if you want their last state
        any_owned_province = {
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
            is_colonial = no
        }
        OR = {
            neighbour = THIS
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = {
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
                THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                civilized = yes
                THIS = {
                    civilized = yes
                }
            }
            AND = {
                civilized = no
                THIS = {
                    civilized = no
                }
            }
        }
        is_vassal = no
    }

    allowed_states = {
        is_colonial = no
        any_owned_province = {
            NOT = { is_core = THIS }
            is_colonial = no
        }
        any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes }
    }

    allowed_states_in_crisis = {
        any_owned_province = {
            any_neighbor_province = {
                owner = { tag = THIS }
            }
        }
    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_TAKE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }
	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}

# Liberate puppet
liberate_puppet = {
    sprite_index = 18
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 12

    construction_speed = 0.3

    badboy_factor = 2.8
    prestige_factor = 2
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 0

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 1
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 1
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 1


    can_use = {
		ai = yes
        NOT = {
            is_our_vassal = THIS
            has_country_modifier = neutrality
			has_country_modifier = neutrality_modifier
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = {
                total_amount_of_divisions = 1
            }
            war_with = THIS
        }
        number_of_states = 2
        THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = neutrality } }
        THIS = { is_greater_power = yes }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = no_more_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { government = fascist_dictatorship }
            THIS = { government = proletarian_dictatorship }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            war_with = THIS
            NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = 0 } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = dismantle_declared }
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = in_great_war } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal is scope
    allowed_countries = {
        FROM = { exists = no }
        OR = {
            is_releasable_vassal = FROM
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        OR = {
            THIS = { ai = no }
            FROM = { NOT = { any_core = { is_core = THIS } } }
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
        }
        NOT = {
            tag = FROM
            FROM = { tag = THIS }
            FROM = { tag = MTC }
            this_culture_union = FROM
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = ETH }
                NOT = { exists = ETH }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { tag = BOL }
                exists = PBC
            }
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = no }
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    OR = {
                        any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS }
                        controlled_by = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                FROM = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    is_core = FROM
                    OR = {
                        any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS }
                        any_neighbor_province = {
                            owner = {
                                OR = {
                                    in_sphere = THIS
                                    alliance_with = THIS
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        controlled_by = THIS
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    continent = europe
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {
                        continent = north_america
                        continent = south_america
                    }
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    OR = {
                        continent = north_america
                        continent = south_america
                    }
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                THIS = { capital_scope = { continent = asia } }
                any_owned_province = {
                    continent = asia
                    is_core = FROM
                }
            }
            AND = {
                THIS = { civilized = yes }
                FROM = { is_culture_group = THIS }
                any_owned_province = { is_core = FROM }
            }
        }
        FROM = {
            OR = {
                is_cultural_union = no
                involved_in_crisis = yes
            }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            FROM = { civilized = yes }
            THIS = { civilized = no }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
        OR = {
            FROM = { involved_in_crisis = yes }
            THIS = { ai = no }
        }
    }

    # THIS - us
    # FROM - country scope is possible match?
    # war target country of goal's state
    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = {
            is_core = FROM
        }
    }
    all_allowed_states = yes
    po_transfer_provinces = yes

    war_name = WAR_LIBERATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                exists = no
                has_country_flag = existing_country
            }
            clr_country_flag = existing_country
        }
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                exists = no
                has_country_flag = vassal_nation_cb
            }
            clr_country_flag = vassal_nation_cb
        }
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.25
        }
    }

    on_po_accepted = {
        country_event = 2651    # Territorial Loss event
        THIS = { country_event = 19369 } # Starts puppeting event chain
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
    }
}

establish_protectorate_casus_belli_no_infamy = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
	constructing_cb = no
    months = 0
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 1
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 5
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 2
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 2
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        civilized = no
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }

    }

    po_annex = yes

    war_name = WAR_PROTECTORATE_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }
    on_po_accepted = { tech_school = unciv_tech_school }
}

demand_concession_casus_belli_no_infamy = {
    sprite_index = 7
    is_triggered_only = yes
    months = 0
	constructing_cb = no
    crisis = no

    badboy_factor = 0
    prestige_factor = 1
    peace_cost_factor = 0.6
    penalty_factor = 1

    break_truce_prestige_factor = 1
    break_truce_infamy_factor = 1
    break_truce_militancy_factor = 1
    truce_months = 48

    good_relation_prestige_factor = 0
    good_relation_infamy_factor = 0
    good_relation_militancy_factor = 0

    always = no

    can_use = {
        OR = {
            AND = {
                OR = {
                    THIS = { total_amount_of_ships = 5 }
                    THIS = { ai = no }
                }
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
            }
            neighbour = THIS
			AND = { OR = { any_neighbor_country = { substate_of = THIS } any_neighbor_country = { vassal_of = THIS } } THIS = { ai = no } }
            AND = { war_with = THIS ai = no }
        }
        NOT = { is_our_vassal = THIS }
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { total_amount_of_divisions = 1 }
        }
        civilized = no
        number_of_states = 2
        OR = {
            war_with = THIS
            THIS = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = punitive_effects } }
        }
    }

    allowed_states = {
        any_owned_province = { is_colonial = no }

        NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_capital = yes } }
        OR = {
            any_owned_province = { any_neighbor_province = { owned_by = THIS } }

			#Player can take any state neighboring their substate
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							substate_of = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}

			#Player can take any state neighboring their satellite
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							vassal_of = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				THIS = { ai = no }
			}
            AND = {
                THIS = { ai = no }
                owner = { war_with = THIS }
            }
            AND = {
                any_owned_province = { port = yes }
                THIS = { any_owned_province = { port = yes } }
            }
        }

    }

    po_demand_state = yes

    war_name = WAR_CONCESSION_NAME

    on_add = {
        move_issue_percentage = {
            from = jingoism
            to = pro_military
            value = 0.1
        }
    }


	on_po_accepted = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = recently_lost_war duration = 1825 }
	}
}
